<h1 _ngcontent-irw-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="@ohos.net.http (数据请求)"> @ohos.net.http (数据请求) </h1>

<div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>本模块提供HTTP数据请求能力。应用可以通过HTTP发起一个数据请求，支持常见的GET、POST、OPTIONS、HEAD、PUT、DELETE、TRACE、CONNECT方法。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>本模块首批接口从API version 6开始支持。后续版本的新增接口，采用上角标单独标记接口的起始版本。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="导入模块" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">导入模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="导入模块" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" 15开始支持该属性。</span></li><li>  },</li><li>  <span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">err: BusinessError, data: http.HttpResponse</span>) =&gt;</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (!err) {</li><li>      <span class="hljs-comment">// data.result为HTTP响应内容，可根据业务需要进行解析。</span></li><li>      <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'Result:'</span> + <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">stringify</span>(data.<span class="hljs-property">result</span>));</li><li>      <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'code:'</span> + function_">stringify</span>(data.<span class="hljs-property">resultType</span>));</li><li>      <span class="hljs-comment">// data.header为HTTP响应头，可根据业务需要进行解析。</span></li><li>      <span class="hljs-property">cookies</span>)); <span class="hljs-comment">// 自API version 8开始支持cookie。</span></li><li>      <span class="hljs-comment">// 取消订阅HTTP响应头事件。</span></li><li>      httpRequest.<span Object。</span></li><li>      httpRequest.<span class="hljs-title function_">destroy</span>();</li><li>    } <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {</li><li>      <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">error</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'error:'</span> + <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">stringify</span>(err));</li><li>      <span class="hljs-comment">// 取消订阅HTTP响应头事件。</span></li><li>      httpRequest.<span class="hljs-title function_">off</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'headersReceive'</span>);</li><li>      <span class="hljs-comment">// 当该请求使用完毕时，开发者务必调用destroy方法主动销毁该JavaScript Object。</span></li><li>      httpRequest.<span class="hljs-title function_">destroy</span>();</li><li>    }</li><li>  });</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>console.info()输出的数据中包含换行符会导致数据出现截断现象。</p>       <p>自API 12开始支持接收经过brotli算法压缩的HTTP响应。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 846px;">     <h2 id="httpcreatehttp" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">http.createHttp<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="httpcreatehttp" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>createHttp(): HttpRequest</p>     <p>创建一个HTTP请求，里面包括发起请求、中断请求、订阅/取消订阅HTTP Response Header事件。当发起多个HTTP请求时，需为每个HTTP请求创建对应HttpRequest对象。每一个HttpRequest对象对应一个HTTP请求。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>当该请求使用完毕时，需调用destroy方法主动销毁HttpRequest对象，否则会出现资源泄露问题。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Communication.NetStack</p>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.8.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.8.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">HttpRequest</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回一个HttpRequest对象，里面包括request、requestInStream、destroy、on和off方法。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { http } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.NetworkKit'</span>;</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> httpRequest = http.<span class="hljs-title function_">createHttp</span>();</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="httprequest" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">HttpRequest<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="httprequest" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>HTTP请求任务。在调用HttpRequest的方法前，需要先通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#httpcreatehttp">createHttp()</a>创建一个任务。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 3306px;">     <h3 id="request" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv" class="firsth2">request<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="request" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>request(url: string, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;HttpResponse&gt;): void</p>     <p>根据URL地址，发起HTTP网络请求，使用callback方式作为异步方法。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>(1) 此接口仅支持接收5MB以内的数据，如果需要接收超过5MB的数据，则需主动在<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#httprequestoptions">HttpRequestOptions</a>的maxLimit中进行设置，或者使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#requestinstream10">requestInStream</a>接口发起流式请求。</p>       <p>(2) 如需传入cookies，请开发者自行在参数options中添加。</p>       <p>(3) 若URL包含中文或其他语言，需先调用encodeURL(URL)编码，再发起请求。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>需要权限</strong>：ohos.permission.INTERNET</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Communication.NetStack</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">url</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">发起网络请求的URL地址。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#httpresponse">HttpResponse</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-net-http">HTTP错误码</a>。</p>     <p>HTTP错误码映射关系：2300000 + curl错误码。更多常用错误码可参考：<a href="https://curl.se/libcurl/c/libcurl-errors.html" target="_blank">curl错误码</a></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">request<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="request-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>request(url: string, options: HttpRequestOptions, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;HttpResponse&gt;):void</p>     <p>根据URL地址和相关配置项，发起HTTP网络请求，使用callback方式作为异步方法。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>(1) 此接口仅支持接收5MB以内的数据，如果需要接收超过5MB的数据，则需主动在<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#httprequestoptions">HttpRequestOptions</a>的maxLimit中进行设置，或者使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#requestinstream10">requestInStream</a>接口发起流式请求。</p>       <p>(2) 如需传入cookies，请开发者自行在参数options中添加。</p>       <p>(3) 若URL包含中文或其他语言，需先调用encodeURL(URL)编码，再发起请求。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>需要权限</strong>：ohos.permission.INTERNET</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Communication.NetStack</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th              <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">url</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">发起网络请求的URL地址。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder"   </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍参见<a certificate error.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">2300059</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">The specified SSL cipher cannot be used.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">2300060</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Invalid SSL peer certificate or SSH remote key.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">2300061</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Invalid HTTP encoding format.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Internal error.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" id="request-2" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">request<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="request-2" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>request(url: string, options? : HttpRequestOptions): Promise&lt;HttpResponse&gt;</p>     <p>根据URL地址，发起HTTP网络请求，使用Promise方式作为异步方法。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>(1) 此接口仅支持接收5MB以内的数据，如果需要接收超过5MB的数据，则需主动在<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#httprequestoptions">HttpRequestOptions</a>的maxLimit中进行设置，或者使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#requestinstream10">requestInStream</a>接口发起流式请求。</p>       <p>(2) 如需传入cookies，请开发者自行在参数options中添加。</p>       <p>(3) 若URL包含中文或其他语言，需先调用encodeURL(URL)编码，再发起请求。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>需要权限</strong>：ohos.permission.INTERNET</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Communication.NetStack</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">url</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">发起网络请求的URL地址。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">HttpRequestOptions</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#httprequestoptions">HttpRequestOptions</a>。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#httpresponse">HttpResponse</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">以Promise形式返回发起请求的结果。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-net-http">HTTP错误码</a>。</p>     <p>HTTP错误码映射关系：2300000 + curl错误码。更多常用错误码可参考：<a href="https://curl.se/libcurl/c/libcurl-errors.html" target="_blank">curl错误码</a></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> id="requestinstream10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">requestInStream<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="requestinstream10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>requestInStream(url: string, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;number&gt;): void</p>     <p>根据URL地址，发起HTTP网络请求并返回流式响应，使用callback方式作为异步方法。</p>     <p><strong>需要权限</strong>：ohos.permission.INTERNET</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Communication.NetStack</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">url</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">发起网络请求的URL地址。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder"    </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍参见<a active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="requestinstream10-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span HttpRequestOptions, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;number&gt;): void</p>     <p>根据URL地址和相关配置项，发起HTTP网络请求并返回流式响应，使用callback方式作为异步方法。</p>     <p><strong>需要权限</strong>：ohos.permission.INTERNET</p> auto 3497px;">     <h3 id="requestinstream10-2" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">requestInStream<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="requestinstream10-2" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>requestInStream(url: string, options? : HttpRequestOptions): Promise&lt;number&gt;</p>     <p>根据URL地址，发起HTTP网络请求并返回流式响应，使用Promise方式作为异步方法。</p>     <p><strong>需要权限</strong>：ohos.permission.INTERNET</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Communication.NetStack</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.13.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.13.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.13.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.13.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">url</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">发起网络请求的URL地址。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">HttpRequestOptions</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#httprequestoptions">HttpRequestOptions</a>。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.13.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.13.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#responsecode">number</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">以Promise形式返回发起请求的结果。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>和<a device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">on("headerReceive")<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onheaderreceivedeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>on(type: "headerReceive", callback: AsyncCallback&lt;Object&gt;): void</p>     <p>订阅HTTP Response Header 事件。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 6开始支持，从API version 8开始废弃，建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#onheadersreceive8">on("headersReceive")<sup>8+</sup></a>替代。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Communication.NetStack</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.14.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.14.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.14.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.14.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">type</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">订阅的事件类型，'headerReceive'。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt;Object&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数。当订阅成功，error为undefined，data为获取到HTTP响应头；否则为错误对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">off("headerReceive")<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="offheaderreceivedeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数。当订阅成功时，回调内容是<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#datasendprogressinfo11">DataSendProgressInfo</a>，订阅失败时为undefined。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 915px;">     <h3 id="offdatasendprogress11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">off('dataSendProgress')<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="offdatasendprogress11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>off(type: 'dataSendProgress', callback?: Callback&lt;DataSendProgressInfo&gt;): void</p>     <p>取消订阅HTTP网络请求数据发送进度事件。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Communication.NetStack</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">type</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">取消订阅的事件类型：'dataSendProgress'。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Callback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#datasendprogressinfo11">DataSendProgressInfo</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数。可以指定传入on中的callback取消对应的订阅，也可以不指定callback清空所有订阅。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 8538px;">     <h2 id="httprequestoptions" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">HttpRequestOptions<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="httprequestoptions" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>发起HTTP请求时，可选配置信息。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Communication.NetStack</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.4.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.4.1.6.1.2" width="20%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.4.1.6.1.3" width="20%">只读</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.4.1.6.1.4" width="20%">可选</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.4.1.6.1.5" width="20%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">method</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#requestmethod">RequestMethod</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>请求方式，默认为GET。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">extraData</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">string | Object | ArrayBuffer</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>发送请求的额外数据，默认无此字段。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong> 没有额外数据时，避免添加该参数；若必须添加，请填写undefined或者null，避免直接传入"。</p>          <p>1. 当HTTP请求为POST、PUT、DELETE等方法时，此字段为HTTP请求的content，以UTF-8编码形式作为请求体。</p>          <p>示例如下：</p>          <p>(1) 当'content-Type'为'application/x-www-form-urlencoded'时，请求提交的信息主体数据必须在key和value进行URL转码后（encodeURIComponent/encodeURI），按照键值对"key1=value1&amp;key2=value2&amp;key3=value3"的方式进行编码，该字段对应的类型通常为String。</p>          <p>(2) 当'content-Type'为'text/xml'时，该字段对应的类型通常为String。</p>          <p>(3) 当'content-Type'为'application/json'时，该字段对应的类型通常为Object。</p>          <p>(4) 当'content-Type'为'application/octet-stream'时，该字段对应的类型通常为ArrayBuffer。</p>          <p>(5) 当'content-Type'为'multipart/form-data'且需上传的字段为文件时，该字段对应的类型通常为ArrayBuffer。</p>          <p>以上信息仅供参考，并可能根据具体情况有所不同。</p>          <p>2. 当HTTP请求为GET、OPTIONS、TRACE、CONNECT等方法时，此字段为HTTP请求参数的补充。开发者需传入Encode编码后的string类型参数，Object类型的参数无需预编码，参数内容会拼接到URL中进行发送。ArrayBuffer类型的参数不会做拼接处理。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">expectDataType<sup>9+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#httpdatatype9">HttpDataType</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>指定返回数据的类型，默认无此字段。如果设置了此参数，系统将优先返回指定的类型。当指定其类型为Object时，最大长度为65536字符数。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">usingCache<sup>9+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>是否使用缓存，true表示请求时优先读取缓存，false表示不使用缓存；默认为true，请求时优先读取缓存。缓存跟随当前进程生效，新缓存会替换旧缓存。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">priority<sup>9+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>HTTP/HTTPS请求并发优先级，值越大优先级越高，范围[1,1000]，默认为1。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">header</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">Object</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>HTTP请求头字段。当请求方式为"POST" "PUT" "DELETE" 或者""时，默认{'content-Type': 'application/json'}， 否则默认{'content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded'}。</p>          <p>如果head中包含number类型的字段，最大支持int64的整数。</p>          <p>header字段支持JSON格式如 <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#完整示例">完整示例</a> 和Record&lt;string, string&gt;格式输入。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">readTimeout</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>读取超时时间。单位为毫秒（ms），默认为60000ms。传入值需为uint32_t范围内的整数。</p>          <p>设置为0表示不会出现超时情况。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">connectTimeout</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>连接超时时间。单位为毫秒（ms），默认为60000ms。传入值需为uint32_t范围内的整数。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">usingProtocol<sup>9+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#httpprotocol9">HttpProtocol</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>使用协议。默认值由系统自动指定。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">usingProxy<sup>10+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">boolean | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-net-connection#httpproxy10">HttpProxy</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>HTTP代理配置，该项不配置时表示不使用代理。</p>          <p>- 当usingProxy为布尔类型true时，使用默认网络代理，为false时，不使用代理。</p>          <p>- 当usingProxy为HttpProxy类型时，使用指定网络代理。当前HttpProxy不支持指定username和password字段。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">caPath<sup>10+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>如果设置了此参数且证书有效，系统将使用用户指定的CA证书和系统预设的CA证书；否则仅使用系统预设的CA证书。CA证书路径为沙箱映射路径（开发者可通过UIAbilityContext提供的能力获取应用沙箱路径）。目前仅支持后缀名为.pem的文本格式证书。</p>          <p>系统预设CA证书位置：/etc/ssl/certs/cacert.pem。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">caData<sup>20+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>如果设置了此参数且证书有效，系统将使用用户指定的CA证书和系统预设的CA证书；否则仅使用系统预设的CA证书。如果同时设置了caPath和caData，caData将被系统忽略。目前仅支持传入.pem格式的证书内容，最大长度为8000字节。仅支持传入单证书，不支持证书链传入。</p>          <p>系统预设CA证书位置：/etc/ssl/certs/cacert.pem。证书路径为沙箱映射路径（开发者可通过UIAbilityContext提供的能力获取应用沙箱路径）。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">resumeFrom<sup>11+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>用于设置下载起始位置，该参数只能用于GET方法，不能用于其他。HTTP标准（RFC 7233第3.1节）允许服务器忽略范围请求。</p>          <p>- 使用HTTP PUT时，不能使用该选项，因为该选项可能与其他选项冲突。</p>          <p>- 取值范围是：[1，4294967296（4GB）]，超出范围则不生效。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">resumeTo<sup>11+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>用于设置下载结束位置，该参数只能用于GET方法，不能用于其他。HTTP标准（RFC 7233第3.1节）允许服务器忽略范围请求。</p>          <p>- 使用HTTP PUT时，不能使用该选项，因为该选项可能与其他选项冲突。</p>          <p>- 取值范围是：[1，4294967296（4GB）]，超出范围则不生效。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">clientCert<sup>11+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#clientcert11">ClientCert</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">支持传输客户端证书。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">dnsOverHttps<sup>11+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置使用HTTPS协议的服务器进行DNS解析。</p>          <p>- 参数必须根据以下格式进行URL编码："https:// host:port/path"。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">dnsServers<sup>11+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">Array&lt;string&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置指定的DNS服务器进行DNS解析。</p>          <p>- 最多可以设置3个DNS解析服务器。如果有3个以上，只取前3个。</p>          <p>- 服务器必须是IPV4或者IPV6地址。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">maxLimit<sup>11+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>响应消息的最大字节限制。</p>          <p>默认值为5*1024*1024，以字节为单位。最大值为100*1024*1024，以字节为单位。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">multiFormDataList<sup>11+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">Array&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#multiformdata11">MultiFormData</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">当'content-Type'为'multipart/form-data'时，则上传该字段定义的数据字段表单列表。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">certificatePinning<sup>12+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#certificatepinning12">CertificatePinning</a> | CertificatePinning[]</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">支持动态设置证书锁定配置，可以传入单个或多个证书PIN码。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">addressFamily<sup>15+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#addressfamily15">AddressFamily</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">支持解析目标域名时限定地址类型。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">remoteValidation<sup>18+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#remotevalidation18">RemoteValidation</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>证书颁发机构（CA），用于验证远程服务器的身份。如果未设置此字段，系统CA将用于验证远程服务器的标识。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 18开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">tlsOptions<sup>18+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#tlsoptions18">TlsOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>TLS配置。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 18开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">serverAuthentication<sup>18+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#serverauthentication18">ServerAuthentication</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>安全连接期间的服务器身份验证配置。默认不认证。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 18开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">sslType<sup>20+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#ssltype20">SslType</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>使用安全通信协议TLS（默认）或TLCP。如果使用TLCP，相关的选项（如caPath、clientCert和clientEncCert）必须赋有效值。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">clientEncCert<sup>20+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#clientcert11">ClientCert</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>支持应用程序传入客户端证书，使服务器能够进行验证客户端的加密身份。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 888px;">     <h2 id="requestmethod" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">RequestMethod<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="requestmethod" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>HTTP 请求方法。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Communication.NetStack</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.5.1.4.1.1" width="33.33333333333333%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.5.1.4.1.2" width="33.33333333333333%">值</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.5.1.4.1.3" width="33.33333333333333%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">OPTIONS</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">"OPTIONS"</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">OPTIONS方法描述了目标资源的通信选项。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">GET</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">"GET"</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">GET方法请求指定资源的表示。使用GET的请求应该只检索数据，不应该包含请求内容。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">HEAD</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">"HEAD"</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">HEAD方法请求与GET请求相同的响应，但没有响应主体。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">POST</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">"POST"</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">POST方法将实体提交给指定的资源，通常会导致服务器上的状态更改。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">PUT</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">"PUT"</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">PUT方法将目标资源的所有当前表示替换为请求内容。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">DELETE</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">"DELETE"</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">DELETE方法用于删除指定的资源。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">TRACE</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">"TRACE"</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">TRACE方法沿到达目标资源的路径执行消息环回测试。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">CONNECT</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">"CONNECT"</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">CONNECT方法建立到由目标资源标识的服务器的隧道。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 4092px;">     <h2 id="responsecode" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">ResponseCode<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i width="33.33333333333333%">501</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>服务器不支持请求的功能，无法完成请求。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">BAD_GATEWAY</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">502</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>充当网关或代理的服务器，从远端服务器接收到了一个无效的请求。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">UNAVAILABLE</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">503</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>由于超载或系统维护，服务器暂时无法处理客户端的请求。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>充当网关或代理的服务器，未及时从远端服务器获取请求。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">VERSION</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">505</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>服务器不支持客户端请求中使用的HTTP协议版本。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>多部分表单数据的类型。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Communication.NetStack</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.4.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.4.1.6.1.4" width="20%">可选</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.4.1.6.1.5" width="20%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">name</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">数据名称。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">contentType</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">数据类型，如'text/plain'，'image/png', 'image/jpeg', 'audio/mpeg', 'video/mp4'等。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">remoteFileName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>上传到服务器保存为文件的名称。</p>          <p><strong>说明</strong>：指定该字段后，请求头中会添加filename字段，表示上传到服务器文件的名称。</p>          <p>（1）当上传数据为文件时，若通过data字段指定文件内容，通常需要设置remoteFileName字段，用以指定上传到服务器文件的名称（实际结果与服务器具体行为有关）；若通过filePath字段指定文件路径，请求头中会自动添加filename字段，其默认值为filePath中的文件名称，如需特殊指定，也可通过本字段对filename重新设置。</p>          <p>（2）当上传数据为二进制格式时，则必须设置remoteFileName字段。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">data</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">string | Object | ArrayBuffer</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">表单数据内容。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">filePath</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>此参数将文件路径指向的文件内容设置为表单数据，如果未指定data内容，则必须设置filePath。</p>          <p><strong>说明</strong>：需传入文件管理模块支持的格式，可以通过文件管理的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-file-fs#fsaccess">access</a>接口，验证文件是否存在且可访问。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 929px;">     <h2 id="httpcreatehttpresponsecache9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">http.createHttpResponseCache<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="httpcreatehttpresponsecache9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>createHttpResponseCache(cacheSize?: number): HttpResponseCache</p>     <p>创建一个HttpResponseCache对象，可用于存储HTTP请求的响应数据。对象中可调用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#flush9">flush</a>与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#delete9">delete</a>方法，cacheSize指定缓存大小。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Communication.NetStack</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">cacheSize</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">缓存大小。最大为10*1024*1024（10MB），默认最大。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#httpresponsecache9">HttpResponseCache</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回一个存储HTTP访问请求响应的对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { http } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.NetworkKit'</span>;</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> httpResponseCache = http.<span class="hljs-title function_">createHttpResponseCache</span>();</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 926px;">     <h2 id="httpresponsecache9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">HttpResponseCache<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="httpresponsecache9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>存储HTTP访问请求响应的对象。在调用HttpResponseCache的方法前，需要先通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-http#httpcreatehttpresponsecache9">createHttpResponseCache()</a>创建一个任务。</p>     <p><strong>响应头中的相应关键字使用</strong></p>     <ul>      <li>       <p><strong>Cache-Control</strong>：用于指定缓存策略，如no-cache, no-store, max-age, public, private等。</p></li>      <li>       <p><strong>Expires</strong>：指定资源的过期时间，格式为GMT时间。</p></li>      <li>       <p><strong>ETag</strong>：用于资源版本标识，客户端可以使用If-None-Match请求头来验证资源是否已更改。</p></li>      <li>       <p><strong>Last-Modified</strong>：指定资源最后修改时间，客户端可以使用If-Modified-Since请求头来验证资源是否已更改。</p></li>      <li>       <p><strong>Vary</strong>：指定哪些请求头的值会影响缓存的响应，用于区分不同的缓存版本。</p></li>     </ul>     <p>使用这些关键字时，服务器端需要正确配置响应头，客户端则需要根据这些响应头来决定是否使用缓存的资源，以及如何验证资源是否是最新的。正确的缓存策略可以显著提高应用的性能和用户体验。</p>     <p><strong>如何设置Cache-Control头</strong></p>     <p>Cache-Control为通用报头，但通常是在服务器端进行的，允许定义一个响应资源应该何时、如何被缓存以及缓存多长时间。以下是一些常用的Cache-Control指令及其含义：</p>     <ul>      <li>       <p><strong>no-cache</strong>：表示在使用缓存前，必须先去源服务器校验资源的有效性。如果资源未变更，则响应状态码为304(Not Modified)，不发送资源内容，使用缓存中的资源。如果资源已经过期，则响应状态码为200(OK)，并发送资源内容。</p></li>      <li>       <p><strong>no-store</strong>：表示不允许缓存资源，每次请求都必须从服务器获取资源。</p></li>      <li>       <p><strong>max-age</strong>：指定缓存的最大时间(以秒为单位)。例如，Cache-Control: max-age=3600表示缓存的有效期为1小时。</p></li>      <li>       <p><strong>public</strong>：表明响应可以被任何对象(包括：发送请求的客户端，代理服务器等)缓存。</p></li>      <li>       <p><strong>private</strong>：表明响应只能被单个用户缓存，不能作为共享缓存(即代理服务器不能缓存)。</p></li>      <li>       <p><strong>must-revalidate</strong>：表示必须在使用缓存前验证旧资源的状态，并且在缓存过期后，需要重新验证资源。</p></li>      <li>       <p><strong>no-transform</strong>：表示不允许代理服务器修改响应内容。</p></li>      <li>       <p><strong>proxy-revalidate</strong>：与must-revalidate类似，但仅适用于共享缓存。</p></li>      <li>       <p><strong>s-maxage</strong>：类似于max-age，但仅适用于共享缓存。</p></li>     </ul>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1166px;">     <h3 id="flush9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv" class="firsth2">flush<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="flush9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>flush(callback: AsyncCallback&lt;void&gt;): void</p>     <p>将缓存中的数据写入文件系统，以便在下一个HTTP请求中访问所有缓存数据，使用callback方式作为异步方法。缓存数据包括：响应头(header)、响应体(result)、cookies、请求时间(requestTime)和响应时间(responseTime)。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Communication.NetStack</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt;void&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数。返回写入结果。当写入成功时，err为undefined，否则为错误对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-irw-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">SslType<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>type SslType = 'TLS' | 'TLCP'</p>     <p>安全通信协议。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.64.6.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.64.6.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'TLS'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示使用TLS安全通信协议，值固定为'TLS'字符串。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'TLCP'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示使用TLCP安全通信协议，值固定为'TLCP'字符串。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>
